    struct list_node *node = malloc(sizeof(struct list_node));
    if (node != NULL) {
      // set the name and definition of the node
      char *token = strtok(buffer, ",");
      if (token != NULL) {
        node->name = strdup(token);
        token = strtok(NULL, ",");
        if (token != NULL) {
          node->definition = strdup(token);
          node->next = NULL;

char *str_dup(char *src) {
    char *dst = malloc(strlen(src) + 1);
    if (dst != NULL) {
        strcpy(dst, src);
    }
    return dst;
}

size_t hash(char *str) {
    size_t hash = 5381;
    int c;

    while ((c = *str++)) {
        hash = ((hash << 5) + hash) + c; /* hash * 33 + c */
    }

    return hash;
}

struct list_node *lookup(char *str) {
    size_t h = hash(str);
    struct list_node *node = hashtable[h % NBUCKETS];

    while (node != NULL && strcmp(node->name, str) != 0) {
        node = node->next;
    }

    return node;
}

struct list_node *install(char *name, char *definition) {
    size_t h = hash(name);
    struct list_node *node = malloc(sizeof(struct list_node));
    if (node == NULL) {
        return NULL;
    }

    node->name = str_dup(name);
    if (node->name == NULL) {
        free(node);
        return NULL;
    }

    node->definition = str_dup(definition);
    if (node->definition == NULL) {
        free(node->name);
        free(node);
        return NULL;
    }

    node->next = hashtable[h % NBUCKETS];
    hashtable[h % NBUCKETS] = node;

    return node;
}

enum boolean undef(char *name) {
    size_t h = hash(name);
    struct list_node *node = hashtable[h % NBUCKETS];
    struct list_node *prev = NULL;

    while (node != NULL && strcmp(node->name, name) != 0) {
        prev = node;
        node = node->next;
    }

    if (node == NULL) {
        return FALSE;
    }

    if (prev == NULL) {
        hashtable[h % NBUCKETS] = node->next;
    } else {
        prev->next = node->next;
    }

    free(node->name);
    free(node->definition);
    free(node);

    return TRUE;
}

void install(const char *key, const char *value)
{
  int index = hash_function(key);
  struct list_node *new_node = create_node(key, value);
  
  if (hash_table[index] == NULL)
  {
    hash_table[index] = new_node;
  }
  else
  {
    struct list_node *temp = hash_table[index];
    while (temp->next != NULL)
    {
      temp = temp->next;
    }
    temp->next = new_node;
  }
}

{
  // hash function implementation
}

{
  // node creation implementation
}

struct list_node *lookup(const char *key, struct list_node *table[], size_t size)
{
  size_t index = hash(key) % size;
  struct list_node *current = table[index];

  while (current != NULL)
  {
    if (strcmp(current->key, key) == 0)
    {
      return current;
    }
    current = current->next;
  }

  return NULL;

        new_node->next = NULL;

            head = new_node;
            tail = new_node;
        } else {
            new_node->next = head;
            head->prev = new_node;
            head = new_node;
